## Module Tree

└── Project — Root module for the project
    ├── Backend — Server-side logic and APIs
    │   ├── Agents — Agent definitions, execution, and management
    │   │   ├── Agent Definitions — Agent configuration definitions
    │   │   │   ├── Context Steps — Functions and interfaces related to agent context steps.
    │   │   │   │   → backend.github.client.core.github-client-internals: Utilizes the internal GitHub client for agent context operations
    │   │   │   │   → backend.github.pr-processing.pr-formatting.pr-formatters: Context steps use PR formatters to structure pull request data
    │   │   │   │   → backend.github.client.repo-utils: Context steps parse repository full names using GitHub repo utilities
    │   │   │   │   → backend.agents.gadgets: Utilizes agent gadgets like ListDirectory for context-aware operations
    │   │   │   │   → backend.agents.execution.agent-core: Reads PR file contents using agent core functionality for context steps
    │   │   │   │   → backend.database.access.db-client: Resolves database path for context-specific data access
    │   │   │   │   → backend.agents.gadgets.github.pr-details: Formats PR check status using PR details gadgets for context display
    │   │   │   │   → backend.agents.gadgets.pm.work-item-gadgets.work-item-helpers: Reads work item details using helpers for context-aware processing
    │   │   │   │   → backend.logging.core-logging: Type/interface dependency (LogWriter)
    │   │   │   │   → backend.agents.execution.backend-integration.backend-adapter: Type/interface dependency (ContextInjection)
    │   │   │   │   → backend.agents.definitions.shared.agent-messages: Imports INITIAL_MESSAGES
    │   │   │   │   → backend.agents.execution.agent-utils.agent-lifecycle.agent-setup: Type/interface dependency (ContextFile)
    │   │   │   │   → backend.core.utilities.system-operations: File-level import dependency
    │   │   │   │   → backend.core.configuration.project-config.config-types: Type dependency (file-level import)
    │   │   │   │   → backend.pm.pm-triggers.trigger-types: Type dependency (file-level import)
    │   │   │   │   → backend.core.configuration.backend-config.system-configuration.misc-utils: File-level import dependency
    │   │   │   │   → backend.github.client.core.github-client-types: File-level import dependency
    │   │   │   │   → backend.github.client.core.github-client-auth: File-level import dependency
    │   │   │   │   → backend.github.pr-processing.pr-formatting.pr-types: File-level import dependency
    │   │   │   ├── Definition Loader — Utilities for loading and managing agent definitions.
    │   │   │   │   → backend.agents.definitions.schema: Validates agent definitions against a schema
    │   │   │   ├── Definition Schema — Schemas and types for agent definitions.
    │   │   │   ├── Shared Utilities — Common utilities and interfaces used across agent definitions.
    │   │   │   │   ├── Agent Capabilities — Utilities for agent capabilities
    │   │   │   │   │   → backend.agents.definitions.loader: Loads agent definitions to determine capabilities
    │   │   │   │   ├── Agent Messages — Utilities for agent message configurations
    │   │   │   │   │   → backend.agents.definitions.loader: Loads and manages agent definitions for message configurations
    │   │   │   │   ├── Agent Profiles — Utilities for managing agent profiles
    │   │   │   │   │   → backend.core.configuration.db-mapping.config-mapper: Imports AgentConfigRow, DefaultsRow, IntegrationRow (+2 more)
    │   │   │   │   │   → backend.agents.definitions.strategies.tool-registries: Imports CONTEXT_STEP_REGISTRY, GADGET_BUILDER_REGISTRY, PRE_EXECUTE_REGISTRY (+2 more)
    │   │   │   │   │   → backend.agents.definitions.shared.agent-capabilities: Retrieves capabilities associated with agent profiles
    │   │   │   │   │   → backend.integrations: Imports extractIntegrationConfigs, IntegrationProvider
    │   │   │   │   │   → backend.security.authentication: Imports resolveAllIntegrationCredentials, resolveAllOrgCredentials
